\li \bd 26\bd* \wg ἀγάπη\wg* \wl agápē\wl* \k నాల్విర జేవున్- (literally meal/feast of the four people but used for a community feast), జేవున- (meal/feast)\k*; a special type of communal meal having particular significance for early Christians as an expression of their mutual affection and concern; \xt $a(MAT 24:12)\xt*
\li \bd 27\bd* \wg ἀγαπητός\wg* \wl agapētós\wl* \k లాడ- (as in an older person loving a younger person, no sexual connotations. Can be used as dear/beloved, lāḍnur), పెర్మ- (general term, no sexual connotations, HIN prem)\k*; pertaining to one who or that which is loved; \xt $a(MAT 3:17)\xt*

\li \bd 200\bd* \wg ἀκρίς\wg* \wl akrís\wl* \k ఈసుల్క్-, జాడి కోడంగ్-\k*; six-legged winged insect characterized by the fact that its third pair of legs is elongated and adapted to hopping; Acrididae family; moves in swarms that migrate to new areas, which they colonize; at other times lives solitary or in small groups; eaten cooked by toasting, grilling, frying, or broiling, though in some places they are also eaten raw; because of their large numbers and swarming characteristics, locusts were a symbol of a vast attacking army against which there was no defense and also a symbol of divine punishment; \xt $a(MAT 3:4)\xt*
